***загон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загон.html>заго́н</a> (12791)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загон.html>заго́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загон.html>заго́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загон.html>заго́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загон.html>заго́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>herding, driving in, rounding up</li>
<li>enclosure</li>
<li>pen, cattle pen</li>
<li>corral</li>
<li>paddock</li>
<li>yard</li></ol>

***загонять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загонять.html>загоня́ть</a> (9272)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гонять.html>гоня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gonjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загонять.html>загоня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagonjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загнать.html>загна́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drive into</li>
<li>to hammer into</li>
<li>to herd into</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sell, to flog</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загонять.html>загоня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagonjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to exhaust, to fatigue; to drive to exhaustion, to drive too hard (a horse)</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:слышать.html>Слы́шал</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:серый.html>Се́рый</a> (Сергей) <a href = vnd.unilang:вчера.html>вчера́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:байка.html>ба́йку</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:загнать.html>загна́л</a></span>! </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>

***загораживать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загораживать.html>загора́живать</a> (13355)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загородить.html>загороди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagorodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загораживать.html>загора́живать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagoráživatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загородить.html>загороди́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to enclose, to shut in, to fence in</li>
<li>to <a href = vnd.unilang:бар.html>bar</a>, to block up, to obstruct, to barricade
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загораживать.html>загора́живать</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagoráživatʹ</b> komú-libo dorógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stand in smb's way; block smb's way</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загораживать.html>загора́живать</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagoráživatʹ</b> komú-libo svet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stand in smb's light</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загородка.html>загоро́дка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zagoródka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́род</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">górod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:городок.html>городо́к</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gorodók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:городской.html>городско́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gorodskój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***загорать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загорать.html>загора́ть</a> (9565)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загореть.html>загоре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagorétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загорать.html>загора́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagorátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загореть.html>загоре́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tan, to suntan, to sunbathe</li>
<li>to acquire a tan</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to idle, to loaf</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загорать.html>загора́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagorátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li>to catch fire</li>
<li>to break out</li>
<li>to be eager <i>(for)</i>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to feel an urge</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загорать.html>загора́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagorátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***загореться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загореться.html>загоре́ться</a> (5943)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загореть.html>загоре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagorétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загореться.html>загоре́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagorétʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загораться.html>загора́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to catch fire
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:загореться.html>загоре́лся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">les <b>zagorélsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">a forest fire started</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to light up, to turn on, to come on <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of a light source</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приборный.html>прибо́рной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:панель.html>пане́ли</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:загореться.html>загоре́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:красный.html>кра́сная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лампочка.html>ла́мпочка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na pribórnoj panɛ́li <b>zagorélasʹ</b> krásnaja lámpočka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a red light <b>lit up</b> on the instrument panel</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загореться.html>загоре́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спора.html>спор</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagorélsja</b> spor</i> ― <span class="e-translation">an argument broke out</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be eager <i>(for)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:загореться.html>загоре́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́той</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идея.html>иде́ей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>zagorélsja</b> étoj idéjej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he got enthusiastic about/over the idea</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:загореться.html>загоре́лись</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó glazá <b>zagorélisʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">his eyes lit up [blazed]</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:загореться.html>загоре́лись</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:желание.html>жела́нием</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:гнев.html>гне́вом</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó glazá <b>zagorélisʹ</b> želánijem (gnévom)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his eyes kindled with desire (anger)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to feel an urge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:загореться.html>загоре́лось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>zagorélosʹ</b> sdélatʹ éto</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he couldn't wait to do it; he felt a burning desire to do it</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:загореться.html>загоре́лось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:туда.html>туда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поехать.html>пое́хать</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">što éto tebé tak <b>zagorélosʹ</b> tudá pojéxatʹ?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">why is it so urgent for you to go there?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загореть.html>загоре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagorétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загородить.html>загороди́ть</a> (12508)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:городить.html>городи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загородить.html>загороди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagorodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загораживать.html>загора́живать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to enclose, to shut in, to fence in</li>
<li>to <a href = vnd.unilang:бар.html>bar</a>, to block up, to obstruct, to barricade
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загородить.html>загороди́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagorodítʹ</b> komú-libo dorógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stand in smb's way; block smb's way</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загородить.html>загороди́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagorodítʹ</b> komú-libo svet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stand in smb's light</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загородить.html>загороди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagorodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загородка.html>загоро́дка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagoródka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загородка.html>загоро́дки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загородка.html>загоро́дки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загородка.html>загоро́док</a></b>)
</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> enclosure</li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:готовить.html>гото́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gotóvitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заготовка.html>загото́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagotóvka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заготовка.html>загото́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заготовка.html>загото́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заготовка.html>загото́вок</a></b>)

***заграждение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заграждение.html>загражде́ние</a> (14380)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заграждение.html>загражде́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagraždénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заграждение.html>загражде́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заграждение.html>загражде́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заграждение.html>загражде́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(action)</i> blocking, obstruction</li>
<li>barrier, obstruction
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инженерный.html>инжене́рное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заграждение.html>загражде́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">inženérnoje <b>zagraždénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">artificial obstacle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проволочный.html>про́волочное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заграждение.html>загражде́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">próvoločnoje <b>zagraždénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">barbed wire entanglement</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:минный.html>ми́нное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заграждение.html>загражде́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mínnoje <b>zagraždénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">mine field</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аэростат.html>аэроста́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заграждение.html>загражде́ния</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">aerostát <b>zagraždénija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">barrage balloon</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***заграница.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заграница.html>заграни́ца</a> (12413)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заграница.html>заграни́ца</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagraníca</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заграница.html>заграни́цы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заграница.html>заграни́цы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заграница.html>заграни́ц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a foreign country or countries, or any territory outside homeland.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уехать.html>уе́хать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заграница.html>заграни́цу</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ujéxatʹ v <b>zagranícu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to leave the home country, to go abroad. <i>The same as the adverb</i>: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уехать.html>уе́хать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заграница.html>заграни́цу</a></span></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кататься.html>ката́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заграница.html>заграни́цам</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">katátʹsja po <b>zagranícam</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go abroad frequently, to travel from one foreign country to another.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:торговать.html>торгова́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заграница.html>заграни́цей</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">torgovátʹ s <b>zagranícej</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to do foreign trade, to trade overseas.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заграница.html>заграни́цей</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bytʹ <b>zagranícej</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<i>as adverb</i>) — to be abroad</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сейчас.html>сейча́с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заграница.html>заграни́цей</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On sejčás <b>zagranícej</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is abroad now.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:зарубежный.html>зарубе́жный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:иноземный.html>инозе́мный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:иностранный.html>иностра́нный</a></li>

***загранпаспорт.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загранпаспорт.html>загранпаспорт</a> (32012)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заграничный.html>заграни́чный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:паспорт.html>па́спорт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagraníčnyj pásport</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, literally "foreign passport" or "passport for abroad".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загранпаспорт.html>загранпа́спорт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagranpásport</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загранпаспорт.html>загранпа́спорта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загранпаспорт.html>загранпаспорта́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загранпаспорт.html>загранпаспорто́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>passport (for traveling)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>In Russia, there are two distinct types of passports: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заграничный.html>заграни́чный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:паспорт.html>па́спорт</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zagraníčnyj pásport</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (i.e. <i>foreign passport</i>) and <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внутренний.html>вну́тренний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:паспорт.html>па́спорт</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vnútrennij pásport</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (i.e. <i>internal or domestic passport</i>). The former is used for traveling abroad and the latter is a standard ID.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загребать.html>загреба́ть</a> (18269)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">загреб-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagreb-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загребать.html>загреба́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagrebátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загрести.html>загрести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rake together</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rake in (money)</li>
<li>to bank (the embers of a fire in a furnace)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загребать.html>загреба́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жар.html>жар</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagrebátʹ</b> žar</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bank the fire</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гребень.html>гре́бень</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">grébenʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гребенка.html>гребёнка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">grebjónka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гребешок.html>гребешо́к</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">grebešók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***загреметь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загреметь.html>загреме́ть</a> (6916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to begin doing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греметь.html>греме́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gremétʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rattle, to thunder</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загреметь.html>загреме́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagremétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греметь.html>греме́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to begin to thunder</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be fired, to get into prison</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загрести.html>загрести́</a> (27511)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грести.html>грести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загрести.html>загрести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagrestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загребать.html>загреба́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rake together</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rake in (money)</li>
<li>to bank (the embers of a fire in a furnace)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загрести.html>загрести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жар.html>жар</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagrestí</b> žar</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bank the fire</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***загривок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загривок.html>загри́вок</a> (11606)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грива.html>гри́ва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gríva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare with <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбородок.html>подборо́док</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podboródok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загривок.html>загри́вок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagrívok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загривок.html>загри́вка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загривок.html>загри́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загривок.html>загри́вков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>nape, back of the neck, scruff of the neck; withers (of a horse)
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1907</b>,  Лидия Дмитриевна Зиновьева-Аннибал (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lydia_Zinovieva-Annibal" class="extiw" title="w:Lydia Zinovieva-Annibal">Lydia Dmitrievna Zinovieva-Annibal</a>),  “<a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%93%D0%BB%D1%83%D1%85%D0%B0%D1%8F_%D0%94%D0%B0%D1%88%D0%B0_(%D0%97%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B2%D1%8C%D0%B5%D0%B2%D0%B0-%D0%90%D0%BD%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%B1%D0%B0%D0%BB)/1907_(%D0%92%D0%A2:%D0%81)70" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Глухая Даша (Зиновьева-Аннибал)/1907 (ВТ:Ё)"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухой.html>Глуха́я</a> Даша</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:трагический.html>Траги́ческий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зверинец.html>звери́нец</a></cite>, page 70 |  translated as  “Deaf Dasha”, in Jane Costlow, transl., <cite>The Tragic Menagerie</cite>, Northwestern University Press, 1999, page 41:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">русла́н <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́л</a> людми́лу. людми́ла <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́ла</a> русла́на. <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:луг.html>лугу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ли</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сплестись.html>сплётшись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шея.html>ше́ями</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:грызть.html>гры́зли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́гу</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:загривок.html>загри́вки</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:довольно.html>дово́льно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:потихоньку.html>потихо́ньку</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:рычать.html>рыча́ли</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> ослы́.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ruslán ljubíl Ljudmílu. Ljudmíla ljubíla Ruslána. Na lugú oní stojáli, spljótšisʹ šéjami, grýzli drug drúgu <b>zagrívki</b> i dovólʹno, potixónʹku, ryčáli, kak ne oslý.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Ruslan loved Liudmila. Liudmila loved Ruslan. They stood in the meadow with their necks intertwined, nibbling each other in the <b>withers</b> and growling in a quiet, contented fashion, quite unlike donkeys.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2005</b>,  Андрей Юрьевич <a href = vnd.unilang:курок.html>Курко́в</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Andrey_Kurkov" class="extiw" title="w:Andrey Kurkov">Andrey Yuryevich Kurkov</a>),  chapter 84, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>Зако́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улитка.html>ули́тки</a></cite>  | <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Penguin_Lost" class="extiw" title="w:Penguin Lost">Penguin Lost</a></cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a léstnicu.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He reached under the table, grabbed the cat by the <b>scruff of the neck</b> and, feeling no pain from her claws just then scratching at his wrist, ***загробный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загробный.html>загро́бный</a> (18486)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроб.html>гроб</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grob</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">coffin; grave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загробный.html>загро́бный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagróbnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> afterlife <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">literally "behind/after the grave"</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загробный.html>загро́бный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagróbnyj</b> mir</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>afterlife</b>, afterworld, underworld</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>afterlife</b> world</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загружать.html>загружа́ть</a> (16409)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загрузить.html>загрузи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagruzítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загружать.html>загружа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagružátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загрузить.html>загрузи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to load <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">something on an automobile or a vessel</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to charge, to feed <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">provide a machine or an electronic device with fuel or electricity</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to boot, to load</li></ol>
